```

- Thin ventral filaments extend gracefully downward like delicate threads
- The overall silhouette creates a PERFECT SYMMETRICAL BEAUTY - like a butterfly or flower when viewed from the side
- Every fin is fully extended showing maximum grace and elegance
- The fish appears to be frozen in the most beautiful moment of a graceful glide

- The fish is positioned in the CENTER with generous black negative space on ALL SIDES (top, bottom, left, right)
- Horizontal positioning: fish occupies the middle 60% of frame width, with 20% black space on left and right
- Vertical positioning: fish centered vertically with equal black space above and below
- The tail fin's arc is the visual anchor point
- Creates a sense of elegant suspension in infinite black space
- Museum-worthy, gallery-quality composition that commands attention
```

```
Use the features from the attached photo to create a half-body portrait of a young woman with long dark brown wavy hair, posing casually by a swimming pool in a moody, tropical outdoor setting. The photo is captured with a high-quality digital camera, exhibiting a professional perspective, dim, diffused evening light, and a casual, playful aesthetic.

Hair Detail
Her long, dark brown wavy hair is wet, sleek, and partially disheveled, suggesting she just got out of the water. It is slicked back off her face, with a few strands clinging to her temples.

Attire
She is wearing a black pullover hoodie with the white "GAP" logo emblazoned across the chest. The hoodie is oversized and pulled down to expose her left shoulder, suggesting a minimalist style of dress underneath. On her lower body, she is wearing baggie black bottoms.

Accessories
Her makeup is subtle but defined, featuring full lips in a neutral or soft berry tone. A faint shimmer or gloss is visible on her lips.

Pose
She is on her back looking back at the camera.  

Camera
The shot is a mid-shot portrait, framed from the top of her head down to her upper thigh, emphasizing her pose and the pool environment. The photo is taken with a high-quality digital camera, exhibiting a professional perspective and dim, diffused outdoor lighting (suggesting early evening or an overcast day). The light creates a soft, slightly dark, and moody atmosphere. The image quality is sharp, capturing the subtle texture of the hoodie and the reflection of the light on the wet pool tiles.

Background Overall Detail

Lush, dark green tropical trees and prominent palm fronds rise into the frame, with the sky appearing dark and overcast. The environment is damp and lush, contrasting with the bright blue water.

The overall image conveys
```

## <a id="prompt-1999296679355224000">AI æ‰‹åŠ¨æ¨¡å¼ï¼šç”¨å…‰å­¦åŸç†ç”Ÿæˆç”µå½±æ„Ÿè‚–åƒ</a> (<a href="https://x.com/gaucheai/status/1999296679355224068" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">gauche</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-12/1999296679355224000_0.jpg" alt="AI æ‰‹åŠ¨æ¨¡å¼ï¼šç”¨å…‰å­¦åŸç†ç”Ÿæˆç”µå½±æ„Ÿè‚–åƒ">

```
digging through the api docs, i found parameters that aren't in the main ui. you can control focal length and aperture values with mathematical precision if you use the json input mode. most users are stuck with the default medium shot look.

i set the lens_focal_length to 85mm and f_stop to 1.2 in the code. the bokeh effect is physically accurate. standard prompts just blur the background randomly. this calculates depth based on the subject distance. it changes the compression of the face completely.

a 35mm lens makes the face look wider. an 85mm lens flattens it out. artists know this. photographers know this. but prompters are ignoring it. if you want your generations to look like cinema, you need to stop thinking in words and start thinking in optics.

manual mode for ai.
```

```
ç¿»é API æ–‡æ¡£åï¼Œæˆ‘å‘ç°äº†ä¸€äº›ä¸»ç•Œé¢ä¸­æ²¡æœ‰çš„å‚æ•°ã€‚å¦‚æœä½ ä½¿ç”¨ JSON è¾“å…¥æ¨¡å¼ï¼Œå°±èƒ½ä»¥æ•°å­¦çº§ç²¾åº¦æ§åˆ¶ç„¦è·å’Œå…‰åœˆå€¼ã€‚å¤§å¤šæ•°ç”¨æˆ·åªèƒ½å›°åœ¨é»˜è®¤çš„ä¸­æ™¯ç”»é¢é‡Œã€‚

æˆ‘åœ¨ä»£ç ä¸­å°† lens_focal_length è®¾ä¸º 85mmï¼Œf_stop è®¾ä¸º 1.2ã€‚äº§ç”Ÿçš„æ•£æ™¯æ•ˆæœæ˜¯ç‰©ç†ä¸Šå‡†ç¡®çš„ã€‚æ ‡å‡†æç¤ºè¯åªæ˜¯éšæœºæ¨¡ç³ŠèƒŒæ™¯ï¼Œè€Œè¿™ç§æ–¹æ³•ä¼šæ ¹æ®ä¸»ä½“è·ç¦»è®¡ç®—æ™¯æ·±ï¼Œå½»åº•æ”¹å˜é¢éƒ¨çš„å‹ç¼©æ„Ÿã€‚

35mm é•œå¤´ä¼šè®©è„¸çœ‹èµ·æ¥æ›´å®½ï¼Œè€Œ 85mm é•œå¤´åˆ™ä¼šå°†å…¶å‹å¹³ã€‚è‰ºæœ¯å®¶çŸ¥é“è¿™ä¸€ç‚¹ï¼Œæ‘„å½±å¸ˆä¹ŸçŸ¥é“è¿™ä¸€ç‚¹ï¼Œä½†æç¤ºè¯ä½¿ç”¨è€…å´å¿½è§†äº†å®ƒã€‚å¦‚æœä½ æƒ³è®©ä½ çš„ç”Ÿæˆç»“æœæ‹¥æœ‰ç”µå½±æ„Ÿï¼Œå°±å¿…é¡»åœæ­¢ç”¨æ–‡å­—æ€è€ƒï¼Œå¼€å§‹ç”¨å…‰å­¦åŸç†æ€è€ƒã€‚
```

## <a id="prompt-1999351093814554600">å®¶ä¹¡çš„æ•°å­—å­ªç”Ÿä¿¯ç°å›¾</a> (<a href="https://x.com/langzihan/status/1999351093814554701" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Kengå“¥</a>)

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-12/1999351093814554600_0.jpg" alt="å®¶ä¹¡çš„æ•°å­—å­ªç”Ÿä¿¯ç°å›¾">

<img src="../..//images/2025-12-12/1999351093814554600_1.jpg" alt="å®¶ä¹¡çš„æ•°å­—å­ªç”Ÿä¿¯ç°å›¾">

```
ğŸ‘‡
# Role Definition
You are a **Geo-Spatial Reality Architect (åœ°ç†ç©ºé—´ç°å®å»ºç­‘å¸ˆ)**. Your goal is to translate a 2D **Google Satellite Screenshot** into a hyper-realistic, high-density **Isometric Digital Twin**.

# Core Competency
**SATELLITE-TO-ISOMETRIC TRANSLATION:**
1.  **Single-Layer Reality:** Unlike historical stacks, this is a **current-state snapshot**. You must capture the *exact* layout, road network, and building density shown in the user's satellite image.
2.  **Regional Inference:** Based on the visual cues (roof colors, road markings, vegetation) and any provided coordinates, you must infer the architectural style (e.g., Tokyo dense residential, American suburbia, European old town) and apply it to the 3D structures.
3.  **Frameless Immersion:** strictly NO maps, NO interface elements, NO pins, and NO flat textures. The result must look like a "SimCity" high-end model or a miniature world coming to life.

# Work Process (Internal "Chain of Thought")
When provided with a **[Satellite Image]** and **[Coordinates/Location Name]**:
1.  **Analyze the Grid:** Identify the main road arteries and block shapes in the image.
2.  **Extrude the Volume:** Mentally "pull" the building footprints up into 3D shapes. Estimate heights based on shadow lengths in the image (skyscrapers vs. low-rise).
3.  **Texture Mapping:** Identify the dominant colors (e.g., grey concrete, red tile roofs, green canopy) and apply them to the prompt.

# Output Format (The Final Prompt)
You will output a single prompt block optimized for **Isometric Reality Reconstruction**:

---
**Prompt Structure:**

**[1. The Composition: Spatial Anchor]**
A **frameless, edge-to-edge** high-angle isometric view of **[Insert Detected Region Style]**. The composition is a **direct 3D reconstruction** of the provided satellite topography. The view shows a **single, cohesive moment in time**, capturing the bustling reality of the location. The ground plane is fully textured, removing all abstract baseplates.

**[2. The Architectural Extrusion]**
**[Analyze the Satellite Image and Fill this Section]:**
* **Layout:** [Describe the specific road pattern: e.g., strict grid, winding cul-de-sacs, or organic river-side roads].
* **Density:** [Describe building density: e.g., tightly packed favela-style, sparse villas with pools, or towering concrete jungle].
* **Key Structures:** [Identify specific landmarks seen in the map: e.g., a school with a running track, a large roundabout, a specific bridge, or a park center].
* **Style:** [Describe the architectural texture: e.g., Showa-era Japanese houses, Haussmann Parisian blocks, or brutalist Soviet apartments].

**[3. The Life & Atmosphere]**
Enhance the realism with lived-in details:
* **Street Level:** Miniature cars conforming to the road direction, visible pedestrian crossings, streetlights.
* **Roof Level:** HVAC units, rooftop gardens, water tanks, or solar panels (depending on region).
* **Nature:** Trees lining the streets, distinct vegetation color (tropical green vs. temperate autumn).

**[4. The Rendering Specs]**
**Isometric projection, diorama aesthetic but hyper-realistic scale.** Tilt-shift photography effect (blurring distant edges), majestic sunlight casting sharp shadows. **Unreal Engine 5 render, claymation texture mixed with photorealism, 8k resolution.** --no UI, map pins, flat map, text, borders, frame --ar 16:9 --stylize 250 --v 6.0

---
```

```
Create an ultra-HD, hyper-realistic digital poster of a floating miniature island shaped like [COUNTRY], resting on white clouds in the sky.
```
